DIRECTORY UPDATES
To assist your Telephone Officer with updating changes to your Organization/Command listings,
it is imperative that you provide changes as they occur in the format required and as specified on
page A7 of this directory. This will help eliminate the untimely backlogs that occur just prior to the
quarterly deadline date. Subscribers failing to submit their requirements in the time frame allotted, will not get their listing in the directory. Don’t let this happen to your Command. Submit your
listings as they occur and avoid the last minute rush.
If there are any questions regarding the information above, contact the Directory Clerk, extension
725-4542, for additional information or guidance.

A1

GENERAL INFORMATION
PURPOSE
This directory is provided to primarily assist in finding base telephone numbers. Its use is expressly for official
business purposes only and is the property of the United States Government. This directory must not be
defaced or removed from offices while it remains the current directory. The lending, giving, selling or copying
of information from this directory for soliciting, mailing lists, or other advertising purposes is prohibited. Directory changes should be forwarded to the Directory Clerk (extension 725-4542). The listings are arranged
alphabetically within each major command, and the index is arranged alphabetically to allow users to find
numbers without knowing which command a particular section belongs. Additional assistance is provided in
the Defense Switched Network Numbers listing.
INSTALLATION AND MAINTENANCE
Only personnel designated by the AC/S, COMM & INFORMATION SYSTEM DEPARTMENT, MCB
are permitted to install, relocate, disconnect, remove or repair telephone equipment or cables. Service will be
immediately disconnected and removed if it is found that unauthorized personnel have, in any manner, tampered with the installation of telephone services. Requests for service are made through the Customer Service
Request (CSR) and Telephone Service Request (TSR) (MCBP-2305/4) via the user’s chain of command to
the AC/S, Communication & Information Systems Department.
SECURITY
Except for secure voice telephones, all instruments are subject to potential compromising of classified information. Communication systems are provided for the transmission of official government information only, and are
subject to communications security monitoring and communications management monitoring at all times. The
use of the Base Communications System shall constitute consent to communications security and management
monitoring in accordance with BO P2000.1 and DOD Directive 4640.1.
TELEPHONE USE
Base telephones are for conducting official business only. Public pay telephones are located throughout the
Base for the convenience of the public, and are owned, operated, and maintained by Pacific Bell Telephone
Company. Misuse of these pay telephones will result in their removal. Toll calls with be authorized by each
section and recorded in a monthly Toll Call Record. Billing information can be obtained by calling extension
725-4509 between 0730-1600. Bills are due by the 22nd of each month, and nonpayment of bills may result
in the disconnecting of telephone service. 48 hours advance notification of service termination is required by
the Billing Clerk (extension 725-4509).
OPERATOR SERVICE
Base telephone operators are instructed to be courteous and respectful. Do not reprimand or enter into conversation with the operator, make complaints to the Chief Operator, extension 725-4359.

A2

CAPABILITIES
All telephone extensions have a class of service assigned to them that defines a specific telephone capability.
Questions as to what class of service is assigned to an extension should be directed to Telephone Systems
Office extension 725-3101. Additionally, each extension is assigned a military precedence. The general classes
of service are listed below:
a. (Official with Defense Switched Network Access) – This service provides official government
business access to the Defense Switched Network, Inter-Base circuits, and to the commercial telephone
system. Local commercial calls are chargeable to each unit and are paid for with appropriated funds.
b. A (Official) – This service provides official government business access to Inter Circuits, Leased
Lines, and to the commercial telephone system. Local community calls are chargeable to each unit and are
paid from appropriated funds.
c.

C (Official Restricted) – This service provides official government access to the Base only.

d. B (Unofficial) – This service provides unofficial access to the local commercial telephone system.
Telephones charges are paid for with non-appropriated funds or by individual users.
1) B-1 – This service provides access to the commercial telephone system, and is paid by the
designated occupant in government owned or leased quarters.
2) B-2 – This service may be restricted to Base or have access to the commercial telephone
system, the service is primarily used by the American Red Cross and other morale, welfare and recreation
activities as provided by NAVCOMPMAN, Vol, III.
3) B-3 – This service provides access to the commercial telephone system for commercial
concerns authorized to conduct business from a fixed location on the Base. This authority must be granted
by a contract or permit issued by the Commanding General, Marine Corps Base.

LONG DISTANCE CALLS
Official commercial long distance calls cannot be made by direct dialing. All commercial long distance calls
will be made through the Camp Pendleton Operator, extension 725-4110 and only from extensions with
Class DSN, A service. Unofficial telephone calls will be completed from Class B service or pay telephones.
Dialing information will be provided by the Base Operator.

A7

INSTRUCTIONS FOR SUBMITTAL OF
TELEPHONE WORK REQUEST
1. Submit a Customer Service Request to AC/S CIS.
2. For relocation of telephone instruments, complete both the remove and install sections. Submit a
completed form (MCBCP 2305/4) for each number requiring work. Show extra telephones or keys
under other equipment.
3. Include complete justification and floor plans on new installations or relocations.
4. Copies of MCB Camp Pen Form, (MCBCP 2305) may be drawn from Self Service, Bldg. 22105.
Requests for service received in any other form will be returned to the originator without action.
5. For further information call CIS Customer Service Desk, ext. 725-7758.

DEFENSE SWITCHED NETWORK INSTRUCTIONS
(DSN)
AUTHORIZED USERS
Use of Defense Switched Network (DSN) is limited to official calls of users with DSN service assigned
to their extension. Users of Classes A, B, and C telephone services are not equipped or authorized to make
outgoing DSN calls.
SECURITY

Defense Switched Network (DSN) is a nonsecure network. Users are reminded that care must be
exercised to protect classified information by not discussing such information over the DSN or alluding to such
Information.
TIME LIMITATION

Users placing DSN calls should limit their calls to that necessary to accomplish business, enabling all
users access to DSN lines.
PRECEDENCE SYSTEM

Military precedence is assigned to each DSN capable extension. A different precedence may be requested from the Marine Corps Base DSN operator. Calls might be preempted by an DSN call of higher
precedence. The military precedences to be utilized within DSN are:
a. FLASH - Flesh precedence is reserved for alerts, warnings, or other emergency actions having
Immediate bearing on national command or area authority.
b. IMMEDIATE - Immediate precedence is reserved for vital communications:
1) That have an immediate operational effect on tactical operations.
2) Which directly concern safety or rescue operations.
3) Which affect the intelligence community’s operational role.
c. PRIORITY - Priority precedence is reserved for calls which require prompt completion for national
defense and security, the successful conduct of war or to safeguard life or property, which do not require
higher precedence.
d. ROUTINE . Routine precedence it reserved for all other official communications.
DIRECTORY ASSISTANCE

Defense Switched Network (DSN) numbers are changing daily. If the user reaches a recording indicating that
the number is not in service, etc. call Camp Pendleton Directory Assistance, extension 725-4111 for the correct
number. If the DSN number is not known, also dial 725-4111 for the desired telephone number.
MINIMIZE CONDITIONS

A MINIMIZE condition may be imposed by the Joint Chiefs of Staff as a communications management measure
because of emergency which requires that only critical communications be made to that area. Calls to such an
area will be limited to those calls assisting in emergency.

110

DIALING PROCEDURE

The following procedures apply for calls made from a class DSN extension:
a. To place DSN calls using the precedence assigned to your extension, users with DSN services on
their extension will dial 8 + 8 and receive a second dial tone. When the second dial tone is received, dial the
desired 7 digit DSN number.
b. To place DSN calls using a precedence different than that assigned to your extension, dial 8 + 0, and
place your call through the operator.
c. To place DSN calls to an overseas number (Pacific Area), dial 8 + 8, wait for the second dial tone, dial
315, then dial the desired 7 digit DSN number. To place DSN calls to the European Area, dial 8 + 8 + 225-7366,
and paw the information to the Command Center Operator.
OFF-NET TELEPHONE CALLS
Off-Net Defense Switched Network (DSN) telephone calls are for use with only official telephone calls. This
service enable users to call an Off-Net switchboard which interfaces with the commercial telephone system
and completes an official call to a subscriber without DSN telephone service.
